  270         din_B_1 <= to_signed(0, 32);
  271       ELSIF rising_edge(clk) THEN
  272         IF enb_1_4_0 = '1' THEN
  273           din_B_1 <= din_B_signed;
  274         END IF;
  275       END IF;
  276     END PROCESS reduced_1_process;
  277   
  278   
  279     -- '<S35>/Signal SpecificationB'
  280     addr_B_unsigned <= unsigned(addr_B);
  281   
  282     -- '<S35>/convertB'
  283     convertB_out1 <= resize(addr_B_unsigned, 16);
  284   
  285     reduced_2_process : PROCESS (clk, reset)
  286     BEGIN
  287       IF reset = '1' THEN
  288         convertB_out1_1 <= to_unsigned(16#0000#, 16);
  289       ELSIF rising_edge(clk) THEN
  290         IF enb_1_4_0 = '1' THEN
  291           convertB_out1_1 <= convertB_out1;
  292         END IF;
  293       END IF;
  294     END PROCESS reduced_2_process;

 3373     -- '<S35>/switch_A'

 3379   
 3380     switch_A2_out1 <= switch_A_out1 WHEN we_B_1 = '0' ELSE
 3381         wr_port1_out1;
 3382   
 3383     -- '<S35>/switch_B'
 3384   
 3385     switch_B_out1 <= ram_out1 WHEN And_out1 = '0' ELSE
 3386         switch_A2_out1;
 3387   
 3388     -- '<S35>/ram'
 3389     ram_process : PROCESS (clk, reset)
 3390     BEGIN
 3391       IF reset = '1' THEN
 3392         ram_out1 <= ram_data;
 3393       ELSIF rising_edge(clk) THEN
 3394         IF enb_1_4_0 = '1' THEN
 3395           ram_out1 <= switch_B_out1;
 3396         END IF;
 3397       END IF;
 3398     END PROCESS ram_process;

 3918     BEGIN
 3919       IF reset = '1' THEN

 3923           convertB_out1_2 <= convertB_out1_1;
 3924         END IF;
 3925       END IF;
 3926     END PROCESS reduced_3_process;
